[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:                File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoi/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/poifs/dev/POIFSDump.jav[0m[1;92ma:19[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m26[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m:import java.io.File;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoi/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/poifs/dev/POIFSDump.jav[0m[1;92ma:98[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m122[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m98[0m[39m:    [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m99[0m[39m:    public static void [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry root, File parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mfor[0m[1;39m([0m[39mIterator<Entry> it = [0m[1;35mroot.getEntries[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;35mit.hasNext[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m101[0m[39m:            Entry entry = [0m[1;35mit.next[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m102[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry instanceof DocumentNode[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m103[0m[39m:                final DocumentNode node = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDocumentNode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m entry;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m104[0m[39m:                final byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m bytes;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m105[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDocumentInputStream is = new [0m[1;35mDocumentInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m106[0m[39m:                   bytes = [0m[1;35mIOUtils.toByteArray[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m107[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m108[0m[39m:                try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream out = [0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mout.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m111[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry instanceof DirectoryEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m112[0m[39m:                DirectoryEntry dir = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mentry;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:                File file = new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m114[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mfile.exists[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mfile.mkdirs[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m115[0m[39m:                    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Could not create directory "[0m[39m + [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m116[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m117[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdir, file[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m118[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m119[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mSystem.err.println[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Skipping unsupported POIFS entry: "[0m[39m + [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m120[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m121[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m122[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Problem Analysis[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mPOIFSDump.dump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry, File[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method directly constructs file [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths using `new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Untrusted POIFS entry names containing “‘..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” segments can[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mescape the intended `parent` directory, triggering a file path traversal.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The root cause is missing path normalization and enforcement that the resolved[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput path remains within the designated dump directory.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Fix Approach[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace all raw `new [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, entryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls with a `java.nio.file.Path`–based workflow:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Resolve the entry name against the base directory.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Normalize the resulting path to collapse “‘..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” and “‘.[0m[35m/[0m[39m” segments.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. Reject any path that does not start with the base directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevents [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     d. Create any necessary parent directories atomically via [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Files.createDirectories`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     e. Write the file or recurse into subdirectories using the validated path.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Step-by-Step Patch Strategy[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `POIFSDump.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m98[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m122[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, modify both branches:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Document Entries[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     i.   Extract and trim the document name:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `String entryName = [0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ii.  Compute base and target paths:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path baseDir = [0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path target = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     iii. Validate traversal safety:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid entry name [0m[32m([0m[32mtraversal detected[0m[32m)[0m[32m: "[0m[39m + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     iv.  Ensure parent directory exists:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     v.   Write the document bytes:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream out = [0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mout.write[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Directory Entries[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     i.   Extract directory name:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `String dirName = [0m[1;35mentry.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ii.  Compute and normalize path:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path baseDir = [0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path targetDir = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdirName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     iii. Validate safety:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mtargetDir.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid directory name [0m[32m([0m[32mtraversal detected[0m[32m)[0m[32m: "[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ dirName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          ```[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     iv.  Create the directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand any parents[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     v.   Recurse with the safe directory:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          `[0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdir, [0m[1;35mtargetDir.toFile[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All original behaviors—reading document streams, writing bytes, recursing into[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubdirectories, skipping unsupported entries—remain unchanged, except that paths [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare now validated.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach does not alter the harness or test code and only touches [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`POIFSDump.java`.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Normalization will remove superfluous “.[0m[35m/[0m[39m” and collapse “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” sequences; valid[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmulti-level names [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwithout traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to work.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If a POIFS entry name is absolute [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., starts with “[0m[35m/[0m[39m”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the `resolve` step [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39myields an absolute `target` that fails the `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` check, causing a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclear `IOException`.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Downstream consumers of `POIFSDump` will see traversal attempts rejected [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than untrusted writes.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References and Similar Patterns[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The same pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`resolve`→`normalize`→`startsWith`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can be found in secure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile upload handlers elsewhere in the codebase. Adopting it here aligns with [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished best practices in Apache POI.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external libraries or harness code are modified; the fix is self-contained [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `POIFSDump`.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn Apache POI fuzzer run under Jazzer terminated with a [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception, reporting a file-path traversal when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdumping POIFS entries to the filesystem. The user’s patch modifies [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`POIFSDump.java`, replacing raw `File`-based writes with a `Path`-based [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitize-and-normalize approach—checking that each resolved path stays within the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended base directory, creating parent directories as needed, and rejecting any [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry or directory whose normalized path escapes that base. After applying the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch, the build fails with two compilation errors in `POIFSDump.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39munresolved [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msymbol `Paths`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and an unrelated generic-cast error in `GenericRecordUtil.java`.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer run on `POIPOIFSDumpFuzzer` called `[0m[1;35mPOIFSDump.dump[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which iterates[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mover POIFS entries.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For each `DocumentEntry`, it reads bytes and writes them via  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mFile[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparent, [0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A specially crafted fuzz input causes a node name containing [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“..[0m[35m/../../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m”, triggering Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich throws `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal`.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace pinpoints the sanitizer at [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and the code in `POIFSDump.main`.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In the import section, `import java.nio.file.Paths;` is removed and replaced with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`import java.nio.file.Path;`.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For `DocumentEntry` nodes, the code now:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Retrieves `entryName = [0m[1;35mnode.getName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.trim[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Converts the `parent` `File` to `baseDir = [0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Resolves and normalizes `target = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Checks `[0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`; throws `IOException` if false.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Creates necessary parent directories: [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Writes bytes to `[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- For `DirectoryEntry`, a similar pattern:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Resolve and normalize `targetDir`.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Check `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Call `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and recurse `[0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdir, [0m              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch leaves other code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnotably earlier uses of `[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Restore and adjust imports in POIFSDump.java for Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m compatibility:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-add `import java.nio.file.Paths;` alongside the existing `import [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjava.nio.file.Path;`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove any references to `[0m[1;35mPath.of[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the incompatible `[0m[1;35mPath.of[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call with `[0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `Path inputPath = [0m[1;35mPath.of[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     to  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        `Path inputPath = [0m[1;35mPaths.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Ensure all other `File` → `Path` conversions use only APIs available under Java [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Calls like `[0m[1;35mFiles.newInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remain valid.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Retain and integrate the directory‐traversal checks introduced in the last [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the `[0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDirectoryEntry root, File parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Compute a base directory `Path baseDir = [0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Resolve and normalize entry names:  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `Path target = [0m[1;35mbaseDir.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mentryName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Verify `[0m[1;35mtarget.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbaseDir[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and throw an `IOException` on failure.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Use `[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtarget.getParent[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before writing or [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecursing.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For the lower‐level `[0m[1;35mdump[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOIFSFileSystem fs, int startBlock, String name, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFile parent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Similarly, compute `Path baseDir = [0m[1;35mparent.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Resolve and normalize the `name` argument, checking for traversal via [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`startsWith`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Create parent directories and write to `[0m[1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Keep the GenericRecordUtil adjustments as they do not affect path logic and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready compile under Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validate the patch by compiling under Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m and running the existing fuzz [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm no `cannot find symbol: method [0m[1;35mof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` errors.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the POIFSDump fuzzer to ensure path‐traversal attempts are blocked and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate entries still dump correctly.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExplanation:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Switching from `Path.of` to `Paths.get` restores Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m compatibility while [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving the robust `Path`‐based API.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The added normalization and `startsWith` guards eliminate directory-traversal by [0m [2m                [0m
